not used now\noutcomes = {\n    'planogram_compliance': 'planogram_compliance',\n    'endcap_display': 'endcap_display',\n    'checkout_display': 'checkout_display',\n    'promo_stand': 'promo_stand',\n    'pos_materials': 'pos_materials',\n    'facings': 'facings',\n    'shelf_width_cm': 'shelf_width_cm',\n}\nresults = []\nfor outcome in outcomes:\n    formula = f'{outcome} ~ C(store_id) + C(product_id) + C(month) + C(rep_id)'\n    model = smf.ols(formula, data=df).fit(cov_type='cluster', cov_kwds={'groups': df['store_id']})\n    # Extract rep coefs, baseline rep 1=0\n    rows=[]\n    coefs=[]\n    for rep in sorted(reps['rep_id'].unique()):\n        term=f'C(rep_id)[T.{rep}]'\n        coef=model.params.get(term, 0.0)\n        se=model.bse.get(term, np.nan)\n        p=model.pvalues.get(term, np.nan)\n        rows.append({'rep_id':rep, 'outcome':outcome, 'coef':coef, 'se':se, 'p':p})\n    results.extend(rows)\n    print('done', outcome)\nres = pd.DataFrame(results).merge(reps, on='rep_id')\n# Recenter coefs within region for each outcome\nres['coef_centered'] = res['coef'] - res.groupby(['region','outcome'])['coef'].transform('mean')\n# standardize within outcome for composite\nres['coef_z'] = res.groupby('outcome')['coef_centered'].transform(lambda s: (s-s.mean())/s.std(ddof=0))\n# Flip signs for bad outcomes? all included are good when higher.\nsummary = res.groupby(['rep_id','region']).agg(\n    mean_z=('coef_z','mean'),\n    n_sig_bad=('p', lambda s: 0),\n).reset_index()\n# more useful: count outcomes where rep is bottom-ranked in region or significantly low vs overall 0? cell_mean\n    rep = v.groupby(['rep_id','region']).agg(mean_resid=('resid','mean'), n=('resid','size'), sd=('resid','std')).reset_index()\n    rep['se'] = rep['sd']/np.sqrt(rep['n'])\n    rep['t'] = rep['mean_resid']/rep['se']\n    rep['p_less'] = stats.t.cdf(rep['t'], df=rep['n']-1)\n    rep['metric'] = col\n    visit_metrics.append(rep[['rep_id','region','metric','mean_resid','p_less']])\nvisit_res = pd.concat(visit_metrics, ignore_index=True)\n\n# Shelf audit residuals within store-product-month\nshelf = pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f) for f in sorted(glob.glob('shelf_audit_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True)\nfor c in ['planogram_compliance','endcap_display','checkout_display','promo_stand','pos_materials']:\n    shelf[c] = shelf[c].astype(int)\nshelf = shelf.merge(visits[['visit_id','rep_id','region','store_id','month']], on='visit_id', how='left')\nmetrics = ['planogram_compliance','endcap_display','checkout_display','promo_stand','pos_materials','facings','shelf_width_cm']\nrows=[]\nfor col in metrics:\n    tmp = shelf[['rep_id','region','store_id','product_id','month',col]].copy()\n    cell_mean = tmp.groupby(['store_id','product_id','month'])[col].transform('mean')\n    tmp['resid'] = tmp[col] - cell_mean\n    rep = tmp.groupby(['rep_id','region']).agg(mean_resid=('resid','mean'), n=('resid','size'), sd=('resid','std')).reset_index()\n    rep['se'] = rep['sd']/np.sqrt(rep['n'])\n    rep['t'] = rep['mean_resid']/rep['se']\n    rep['p_less'] = stats.t.cdf(rep['t'], df=rep['n']-1)\n    rep['metric'] = col\n    rows.append(rep[['rep_id','region','metric','mean_resid','p_less']])\nres = pd.concat(rows + [visit_res], ignore_index=True)\n# Standardize mean residual signs: higher better for all included metrics\nres['z'] = res.groupby('metric')['mean_resid'].transform(lambda s: (s-s.mean())/s.std(ddof=0))\nsummary = res.groupby(['rep_id','region']).agg(\n    avg_z=('z','mean'),\n    sig_bad_count=('p_less', lambda s: int((s<0.05).sum())),\n    any_metric_count=('metric','size')\n).reset_index()\n# region-wise ranks\nsummary['rank'] = summary.groupby('region')['avg_z'].rank(method='min')\nprint('Top worst by residual execution composite:')\nprint(summary.sort_values('avg_z').head(30).to_string(index=False))\nprint('\\\\nWorst by region:')\nprint(summary.loc[summary.groupby('region')['avg_z'].idxmin()].sort_values('avg_z').to_string(index=False))\n# show detailed metrics for extreme reps\nworst_ids = summary.sort_values('avg_z').head(12)['rep_id'].tolist()\nprint('\\\\nDetailed metrics for top worst:')\nprint(res[res.rep_id.isin(worst_ids)].sort_values(['rep_id','metric'])[['rep_id','region','metric','mean_resid','z','p_less']].to_string(index=False))\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}

means\n    rep_means = df.groupby(['region','rep_id'])['value'].agg(['mean','count','std']).reset_index()\n    rep_means['region_mean_of_means'] = rep_means['region_mean_of_means']) / rep_means['region_sd_of_means']\n    rep_means['metric'] = metric\n    summary_rows.append(rep_means[['region','rep_id','metric','mean','z']])\nsummary = worse on average corresponding to quality index sign\n# if pc1 correlates positively with simple average, flip if needed\nsimple = out[feat_cols].mean(axis=1)\nif np.corrcoef(out['pc1'], simple)[0,1] < 0:\n    out['pc1'] *= -1\n\n# Gaussian mixture 2 components on pc1/simple features\nZ = out[['pc1']].values\nbest = GaussianMixture(n_components=2, random_state=0).fit(Z)\nlabels = best.predict(Z)\nmeans = pd.Series(best.means_.ravel())\nlow_label = means.idxmin()\nout['gmm_low'] = labels==low_label\n\n# KMeans 2 clusters on X\nkm = KMeans(n_clusters=2, random_state=0, n_init=20).fit(X)\nkm_centers = km.cluster_centers_.mean(axis=1)\nlow_k = km_centers.argmin()\nout['kmeans_low'] = km.labels_==low_k\n\nout['simple_avg'] = simple\nprint('GMM low cluster reps:', out[out.gmm_low].sort_values('pc1')[['rep_id','region','pc1','simple_avg']].to_string(index=False))\nprint('\\\\nKMeans low cluster reps:', out[out.kmeans_low].sort_values('pc1')[['rep_id','region','pc1','simple_avg']].to_string(index=False))\nprint('\\\\nLowest by
